SubProgram "opengl " {
"!!GLSL#version 120

#ifdef VERTEX
uniform vec4 _ProjectionParams;



varying vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
void main ()
{
  vec4 tmpvar_1;
  mat3 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2[0] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_2[1] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_2[2] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[2].xyz;
  tmpvar_1.xyz = normalize((tmpvar_2 * gl_Normal));
  tmpvar_1.w = -(((gl_ModelViewMatrix * gl_Vertex).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (gl_ModelViewProjectionMatrix * gl_Vertex);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
varying vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
void main ()
{
  vec4 enc_1;
  vec2 enc_2;
  enc_2 = (xlv_TEXCOORD0.xy / (xlv_TEXCOORD0.z + 1.0));
  enc_2 = (enc_2 / 1.7777);
  enc_2 = ((enc_2 * 0.5) + 0.5);
  enc_1.xy = enc_2;
  vec2 enc_3;
  vec2 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = fract((vec2(1.0, 255.0) * xlv_TEXCOORD0.w));
  enc_3.y = tmpvar_4.y;
  enc_3.x = (tmpvar_4.x - (tmpvar_4.y * 0.003921569));
  enc_1.zw = enc_3;
  gl_FragData[0] = enc_1;
}


#endif
"
}
SubProgram "d3d9 " {
Bind "vertex" Vertex
Bind "normal" Normal
Matrix 7 [glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0] 3
Matrix 4 [glstate_matrix_modelview0] 3
Matrix 0 [glstate_matrix_mvp]
Vector 10 [_ProjectionParams]
"vs_2_0
dcl_position v0
dcl_normal v1
dp4 oPos.x, c0, v0
dp4 oPos.y, c1, v0
dp4 oPos.z, c2, v0
dp4 oPos.w, c3, v0
dp3 r0.x, c7, v1
dp3 r0.y, c8, v1
dp3 r0.z, c9, v1
dp3 r0.w, r0, r0
rsq r0.w, r0.w
mul oT0.xyz, r0.w, r0
dp4 r0.x, c6, v0
mul r0.x, r0.x, c10.w
mov oT0.w, -r0.x

"
}

{
  highp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  highp mat3 tmpvar_2;

  tmpvar_2[2] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz;

  tmpvar_1.w = -(((glstate_matrix_modelview0 * _glesVertex).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (glstate_matrix_mvp * _glesVertex);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = tmpvar_1;

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  highp vec4 enc_2;
  highp vec2 enc_3;
  enc_3 = (xlv_TEXCOORD0.xy / (xlv_TEXCOORD0.z + 1.0));
  enc_3 = (enc_3 / 1.7777);
  enc_3 = ((enc_3 * 0.5) + 0.5);

  tmpvar_1 = enc_2;
  gl_FragData[0] = tmpvar_1;

#endif

SubProgram "gles3 " {
"!!GLES3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;
uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DeltaTime;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ScreenParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ZBufferParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_CameraWorldClipPlanes[6];
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraProjection;
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosY0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosZ0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_4LightAtten0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightColor[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightPosition[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightAtten[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpotDirection[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor0;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor1;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor2;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor3;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[4];
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightShadowBias;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsNear;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp float t3;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 16
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 17
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 18
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 19
    //MAD
    gl_Position = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 20
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 21
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 22
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 23
    //DP3
    t3 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 24
    //RSQ
    t3 = inversesqrt(t3);
    //Instruction 25
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xyz = vec3(t3) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 26
    //MUL
    t0.x = in_POSITION0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 27
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * in_POSITION0.x + t0.x;
    //Instruction 28
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * in_POSITION0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 29
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z * in_POSITION0.w + t0.x;
    //Instruction 30
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 31
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 32
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec2 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 7
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD0.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 8
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 9
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 10
    //MUL
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 11
    //FRC
    t1.xy = fract(t1.xy);
    //Instruction 12
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t1.y) * 0.003922 + t1.x;
    //Instruction 13
    //MOV
    t0.w = t1.y;
    //Instruction 14
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 15
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}

SubProgram "gles3 " {
"!!GLES3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;

uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;

uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;

uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	lowp float _Cutoff;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _Color;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
highp vec4 t0;
highp float t3;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 13
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 14
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 15
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 16
    //MAD
    gl_Position = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 17
    //MAD
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    //Instruction 18
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 19
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 20
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 21
    //DP3
    t3 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 22
    //RSQ
    t3 = inversesqrt(t3);
    //Instruction 23
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t3) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 24
    //MUL
    t0.x = in_POSITION0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 25
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * in_POSITION0.x + t0.x;
    //Instruction 26
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * in_POSITION0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 27
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z * in_POSITION0.w + t0.x;
    //Instruction 28
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 29
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 30
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif

uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	lowp float _Cutoff;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _Color;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
lowp float t10_0;
bool tb0;
lowp float t10_1;
highp vec2 t2;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 0
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    //Instruction 1
    //MAD
    t10_1 = t10_0 * _Color.w + (-_Cutoff);
    //Instruction 2
    //LT
    tb0 = t10_1<0.0;
    //Instruction 3
    //DISCARD
    if((int(tb0))!=0){discard;}
    //Instruction 4
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 5
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 6
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 7
    //MUL
    t2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 8
    //FRC
    t2.xy = fract(t2.xy);
    //Instruction 9
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t2.y) * 0.003922 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 10
    //MOV
    t0.w = t2.y;
    //Instruction 11
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 12
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"

{
    //Instruction 19
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 20

    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 21

    //Instruction 25
    //MAD

    //Instruction 26

    //Instruction 27

    t3 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 28
    //RSQ
    t3 = inversesqrt(t3);
    //Instruction 29
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t3) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 30
    //MUL
    t0.x = in_POSITION0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 31
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * in_POSITION0.x + t0.x;
    //Instruction 32
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * in_POSITION0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 33
    //MAD

    //Instruction 34

    //Instruction 35
    //MOV

    //Instruction 36
    //RET
    return;

SubShader { 
 Tags { "RenderType"="TreeBark" }
 Pass {
  Tags { "RenderType"="TreeBark" }
  GpuProgramID 171880
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "opengl " {
"!!GLSL#version 120

#ifdef VERTEX
uniform vec4 _Time;
uniform vec4 _ProjectionParams;



uniform mat4 _Object2World;
uniform vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform float _SquashAmount;
uniform vec4 _Wind;
varying vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  vec4 tmpvar_1;
  vec4 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2.w = gl_Vertex.w;
  tmpvar_2.xyz = (gl_Vertex.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz);
  vec4 pos_3;
  pos_3.w = tmpvar_2.w;
  vec3 bend_4;
  vec4 v_5;
  v_5.x = _Object2World[0].w;
  v_5.y = _Object2World[1].w;
  v_5.z = _Object2World[2].w;
  v_5.w = _Object2World[3].w;
  float tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6 = (dot (v_5.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0)) + gl_Color.x);
  vec2 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7.x = dot (tmpvar_2.xyz, vec3((gl_Color.y + tmpvar_6)));
  tmpvar_7.y = tmpvar_6;
  vec4 tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = abs(((
    fract((((
      fract(((_Time.yy + tmpvar_7).xxyy * vec4(1.975, 0.793, 0.375, 0.193)))
     * 2.0) - 1.0) + 0.5))
   * 2.0) - 1.0));
  vec4 tmpvar_9;
  tmpvar_9 = ((tmpvar_8 * tmpvar_8) * (3.0 - (2.0 * tmpvar_8)));
  vec2 tmpvar_10;
  tmpvar_10 = (tmpvar_9.xz + tmpvar_9.yw);
  bend_4.xz = ((gl_Color.y * 0.1) * gl_Normal).xz;
  bend_4.y = (gl_MultiTexCoord1.y * 0.3);
  pos_3.xyz = (tmpvar_2.xyz + ((
    (tmpvar_10.xyx * bend_4)
   + 
    ((_Wind.xyz * tmpvar_10.y) * gl_MultiTexCoord1.y)
  ) * _Wind.w));
  pos_3.xyz = (pos_3.xyz + (gl_MultiTexCoord1.x * _Wind.xyz));
  vec4 tmpvar_11;
  tmpvar_11.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_11.xyz = mix ((pos_3.xyz - (
    (dot (_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, pos_3.xyz) + _SquashPlaneNormal.w)
   * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz)), pos_3.xyz, vec3(_SquashAmount));
  tmpvar_2 = tmpvar_11;
  mat3 tmpvar_12;
  tmpvar_12[0] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_12[1] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_12[2] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[2].xyz;
  tmpvar_1.xyz = normalize((tmpvar_12 * normalize(gl_Normal)));
  tmpvar_1.w = -(((gl_ModelViewMatrix * tmpvar_11).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (gl_ModelViewProjectionMatrix * tmpvar_11);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = gl_MultiTexCoord0.xy;
  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
varying vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  vec4 enc_1;
  vec2 enc_2;
  enc_2 = (xlv_TEXCOORD1.xy / (xlv_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0));
  enc_2 = (enc_2 / 1.7777);
  enc_2 = ((enc_2 * 0.5) + 0.5);
  enc_1.xy = enc_2;
  vec2 enc_3;
  vec2 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = fract((vec2(1.0, 255.0) * xlv_TEXCOORD1.w));
  enc_3.y = tmpvar_4.y;
  enc_3.x = (tmpvar_4.x - (tmpvar_4.y * 0.003921569));
  enc_1.zw = enc_3;
  gl_FragData[0] = enc_1;
}


#endif
"
}

SubProgram "gles " {
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesColor;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord1;
uniform highp vec4 _Time;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform highp mat4 _Object2World;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform highp vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform highp float _SquashAmount;
uniform highp vec4 _Wind;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1 = _glesColor;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_2;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_3;
  tmpvar_3.w = _glesVertex.w;
  tmpvar_3.xyz = (_glesVertex.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4.xy = tmpvar_1.xy;
  tmpvar_4.zw = _glesMultiTexCoord1.xy;
  highp vec4 pos_5;
  pos_5.w = tmpvar_3.w;
  highp vec3 bend_6;
  highp vec4 v_7;
  v_7.x = _Object2World[0].w;
  v_7.y = _Object2World[1].w;
  v_7.z = _Object2World[2].w;
  v_7.w = _Object2World[3].w;
  highp float tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = (dot (v_7.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0)) + tmpvar_4.x);
  highp vec2 tmpvar_9;
  tmpvar_9.x = dot (tmpvar_3.xyz, vec3((tmpvar_4.y + tmpvar_8)));
  tmpvar_9.y = tmpvar_8;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_10;
  tmpvar_10 = abs(((
    fract((((
      fract(((_Time.yy + tmpvar_9).xxyy * vec4(1.975, 0.793, 0.375, 0.193)))
     * 2.0) - 1.0) + 0.5))
   * 2.0) - 1.0));
  highp vec4 tmpvar_11;
  tmpvar_11 = ((tmpvar_10 * tmpvar_10) * (3.0 - (2.0 * tmpvar_10)));
  highp vec2 tmpvar_12;
  tmpvar_12 = (tmpvar_11.xz + tmpvar_11.yw);
  bend_6.xz = ((tmpvar_4.y * 0.1) * _glesNormal).xz;
  bend_6.y = (_glesMultiTexCoord1.y * 0.3);
  pos_5.xyz = (tmpvar_3.xyz + ((
    (tmpvar_12.xyx * bend_6)
   + 
    ((_Wind.xyz * tmpvar_12.y) * _glesMultiTexCoord1.y)
  ) * _Wind.w));
  pos_5.xyz = (pos_5.xyz + (_glesMultiTexCoord1.x * _Wind.xyz));
  highp vec4 tmpvar_13;
  tmpvar_13.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_13.xyz = mix ((pos_5.xyz - (
    (dot (_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, pos_5.xyz) + _SquashPlaneNormal.w)
   * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz)), pos_5.xyz, vec3(_SquashAmount));
  tmpvar_3 = tmpvar_13;
  highp mat3 tmpvar_14;
  tmpvar_14[0] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_14[1] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_14[2] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz;
  tmpvar_2.xyz = normalize((tmpvar_14 * normalize(_glesNormal)));
  tmpvar_2.w = -(((glstate_matrix_modelview0 * tmpvar_13).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (glstate_matrix_mvp * tmpvar_13);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = _glesMultiTexCoord0.xy;
  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = tmpvar_2;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  highp vec4 enc_2;
  highp vec2 enc_3;
  enc_3 = (xlv_TEXCOORD1.xy / (xlv_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0));
  enc_3 = (enc_3 / 1.7777);
  enc_3 = ((enc_3 * 0.5) + 0.5);
  enc_2.xy = enc_3;
  highp vec2 enc_4;
  highp vec2 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5 = fract((vec2(1.0, 255.0) * xlv_TEXCOORD1.w));
  enc_4.y = tmpvar_5.y;
  enc_4.x = (tmpvar_5.x - (tmpvar_5.y * 0.003921569));
  enc_2.zw = enc_4;
  tmpvar_1 = enc_2;
  gl_FragData[0] = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
"
}

uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;

uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;

uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;

uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;

uniform 	lowp vec4 _LightColor0;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _SpecColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightGammaCorrectionConsts;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _WavingTint;
uniform 	vec4 _WaveAndDistance;
uniform 	vec4 _CameraPosition;
uniform 	vec3 _CameraRight;
uniform 	vec3 _CameraUp;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _TreeInstanceColor;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform 	mat4 _TerrainEngineBendTree;
uniform 	vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform 	float _SquashAmount;
uniform 	vec3 _TreeBillboardCameraRight;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraUp;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraFront;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardDistances;
uniform 	vec4 _Wind;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _Color;
uniform 	lowp vec3 _TranslucencyColor;
uniform 	lowp float _TranslucencyViewDependency;
uniform 	mediump float _ShadowStrength;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 in_TEXCOORD1;
in lowp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
highp vec4 t2;
highp vec3 t3;
highp float t4;
highp float t8;
highp float t12;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 40
    //MOV
    t0.x = _Object2World[0].w;
    //Instruction 41
    //MOV
    t0.y = _Object2World[1].w;
    //Instruction 42
    //MOV
    t0.z = _Object2World[2].w;
    //Instruction 43
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0));
    //Instruction 44
    //ADD
    t0.y = t0.x + in_COLOR0.x;
    //Instruction 45
    //ADD
    t8 = t0.y + in_COLOR0.y;
    //Instruction 46
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz;
    //Instruction 47
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t1.xyz, vec3(t8));
    //Instruction 48
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxyy + _Time.yyyy;
    //Instruction 49
    //MUL
    t0 = t0 * vec4(1.975000, 0.793000, 0.375000, 0.193000);
    //Instruction 50
    //FRC
    t0 = fract(t0);
    //Instruction 51
    //MAD
    t0 = t0 * vec4(2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000) + vec4(-0.500000, -0.500000, -0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 52
    //FRC
    t0 = fract(t0);
    //Instruction 53
    //MAD
    t0 = t0 * vec4(2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000) + vec4(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 54
    //MUL
    t2 = abs(t0) * abs(t0);
    //Instruction 55
    //MAD
    t0 = -abs(t0) * vec4(2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000) + vec4(3.000000, 3.000000, 3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 56
    //MUL
    t0 = t0 * t2;
    //Instruction 57
    //ADD
    t0.xy = vec2(t0.y + t0.x, t0.w + t0.z);
    //Instruction 58
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * _Wind.xyz;
    //Instruction 59
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t2.xyz * in_TEXCOORD1.yyy;
    //Instruction 60
    //MUL
    t3.y = t0.y * in_TEXCOORD1.y;
    //Instruction 61
    //MUL
    t4 = in_COLOR0.y * 0.100000;
    //Instruction 62
    //MUL
    t3.xz = vec2(t4) * in_NORMAL0.xz;
    //Instruction 63
    //MOV
    t0.z = 0.300000;
    //Instruction 64
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = t0.xzx * t3.xyz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 65
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz * _Wind.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 66
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = in_TEXCOORD1.xxx * _Wind.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 67
    //DP3
    t12 = dot(_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 68
    //ADD
    t12 = t12 + _SquashPlaneNormal.w;
    //Instruction 69
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-vec3(t12)) * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 70
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 71
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = vec3(_SquashAmount) * t0.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 72
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 73
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 74
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 75
    //ADD
    gl_Position = t1 + glstate_matrix_mvp[3];
    //Instruction 76
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 77
    //MUL
    t4 = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 78
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t0.x + t4;
    //Instruction 79
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 80
    //ADD
    t0.x = t0.x + glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z;
    //Instruction 81
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 82
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 83
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, in_NORMAL0.xyz);
    //Instruction 84
    //RSQ
    t0.x = inversesqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 85
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = t0.xxx * in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 86
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 87
    //MAD
    t0.xyw = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 88
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * t0.zzz + t0.xyw;
    //Instruction 89
    //DP3
    t12 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 90
    //RSQ
    t12 = inversesqrt(t12);
    //Instruction 91
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t12) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 92
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec2 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 31
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 32
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 33
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 34
    //MUL
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 35
    //FRC
    t1.xy = fract(t1.xy);
    //Instruction 36
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t1.y) * 0.003922 + t1.x;
    //Instruction 37
    //MOV
    t0.w = t1.y;
    //Instruction 38
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 39
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"

SubProgram "gles3 " {
"!!GLES3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;
uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DeltaTime;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ScreenParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ZBufferParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_CameraWorldClipPlanes[6];
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraProjection;
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosY0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosZ0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_4LightAtten0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightColor[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightPosition[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightAtten[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpotDirection[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor0;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor1;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor2;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor3;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[4];
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightShadowBias;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsNear;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _LightColor0;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _SpecColor;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightGammaCorrectionConsts;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _WavingTint;
uniform 	vec4 _WaveAndDistance;
uniform 	vec4 _CameraPosition;
uniform 	vec3 _CameraRight;
uniform 	vec3 _CameraUp;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _TreeInstanceColor;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform 	mat4 _TerrainEngineBendTree;
uniform 	vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform 	float _SquashAmount;
uniform 	vec3 _TreeBillboardCameraRight;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraUp;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraFront;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardDistances;
uniform 	vec4 _Wind;
uniform 	lowp vec4 _Color;
uniform 	lowp vec3 _TranslucencyColor;
uniform 	lowp float _TranslucencyViewDependency;
uniform 	mediump float _ShadowStrength;
uniform 	lowp float _Cutoff;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec4 in_TEXCOORD1;
in lowp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
highp vec3 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
highp vec4 t2;
highp vec4 t3;
highp vec4 t4;
highp float t5;
highp float t10;
highp float t15;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 13
    //MOV
    t0.x = _Object2World[0].w;
    //Instruction 14
    //MOV
    t0.y = _Object2World[1].w;
    //Instruction 15
    //MOV
    t0.z = _Object2World[2].w;
    //Instruction 16
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0));
    //Instruction 17
    //ADD
    t0.y = t0.x + in_COLOR0.x;
    //Instruction 18
    //ADD
    t10 = t0.y + in_COLOR0.y;
    //Instruction 19
    //DP2
    t1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xy, glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xy);
    //Instruction 20
    //DP2
    t1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xy, glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xy);
    //Instruction 21
    //DP2
    t1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xy, glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xy);
    //Instruction 22
    //ADD
    t15 = -abs(in_TANGENT0.w) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 23
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = t1.xyz * vec3(t15) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    //Instruction 24
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz;
    //Instruction 25
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t1.xyz, vec3(t10));
    //Instruction 26
    //ADD
    t2 = t0.xxyy + _Time.yyyy;
    //Instruction 27
    //MUL
    t2 = t2 * vec4(1.975000, 0.793000, 0.375000, 0.193000);
    //Instruction 28
    //FRC
    t2 = fract(t2);
    //Instruction 29
    //MAD
    t2 = t2 * vec4(2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000) + vec4(-0.500000, -0.500000, -0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 30
    //FRC
    t2 = fract(t2);
    //Instruction 31
    //MAD
    t2 = t2 * vec4(2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000) + vec4(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 32
    //MUL
    t3 = abs(t2) * abs(t2);
    //Instruction 33
    //MAD
    t2 = -abs(t2) * vec4(2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000) + vec4(3.000000, 3.000000, 3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 34
    //MUL
    t2 = t2 * t3;
    //Instruction 35
    //ADD
    t0.xy = vec2(t2.y + t2.x, t2.w + t2.z);
    //Instruction 36
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * _Wind.xyz;
    //Instruction 37
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t2.xyz * in_TEXCOORD1.yyy;
    //Instruction 38
    //MUL
    t3.y = t0.y * in_TEXCOORD1.y;
    //Instruction 39
    //DP3
    t4.w = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[3].xyz);
    //Instruction 40
    //DP3
    t4.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz);
    //Instruction 41
    //DP3
    t4.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz);
    //Instruction 42
    //DP3
    t4.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 43
    //DP4
    t5 = dot(t4, t4);
    //Instruction 44
    //RSQ
    t5 = inversesqrt(t5);
    //Instruction 45
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = t4.xyz * vec3(t5) + (-in_NORMAL0.xyz);
    //Instruction 46
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = vec3(t15) * t4.xyz + in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 47
    //MUL
    t5 = in_COLOR0.y * 0.100000;
    //Instruction 48
    //MUL
    t3.xz = t4.xz * vec2(t5);
    //Instruction 49
    //MOV
    t0.z = 0.300000;
    //Instruction 50
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = t0.xzx * t3.xyz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 51
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz * _Wind.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 52
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = in_TEXCOORD1.xxx * _Wind.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 53
    //DP3
    t15 = dot(_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 54
    //ADD
    t15 = t15 + _SquashPlaneNormal.w;
    //Instruction 55
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-vec3(t15)) * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 56
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 57
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = vec3(_SquashAmount) * t0.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 58
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 59
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 60
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 61
    //ADD
    gl_Position = t1 + glstate_matrix_mvp[3];
    //Instruction 62
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 63
    //DP3
    t15 = dot(t4.xyz, t4.xyz);
    //Instruction 64
    //RSQ
    t15 = inversesqrt(t15);
    //Instruction 65
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = vec3(t15) * t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 66
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t1.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 67
    //MAD
    t1.xyw = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * t1.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 68
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * t1.zzz + t1.xyw;
    //Instruction 69
    //DP3
    t15 = dot(t1.xyz, t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 70
    //RSQ
    t15 = inversesqrt(t15);
    //Instruction 71
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t15) * t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 72
    //MUL
    t5 = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 73
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t0.x + t5;
    //Instruction 74
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 75
    //ADD
    t0.x = t0.x + glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z;
    //Instruction 76
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 77
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 78
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif

uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
lowp float t10_0;
bool tb0;
mediump float t16_1;
highp vec2 t2;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 0
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    //Instruction 1
    //ADD
    t16_1 = t10_0 + (-_Cutoff);
    //Instruction 2
    //LT
    tb0 = t16_1<0.0;
    //Instruction 3
    //DISCARD
    if((int(tb0))!=0){discard;}
    //Instruction 4
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 5
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 6
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 7
    //MUL
    t2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 8
    //FRC
    t2.xy = fract(t2.xy);
    //Instruction 9
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t2.y) * 0.003922 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 10
    //MOV
    t0.w = t2.y;
    //Instruction 11
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 12
    //RET
    return;
}

"

out vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

    t2 = fract(t2);

    //Instruction 126

    t2 = t2 * t3;

    //Instruction 137

    t5 = inversesqrt(t5);

    //Instruction 153

    //MOV

    //DP3

    //MAD

    //Instruction 161
    //MAD

    //Instruction 162
    //DP3
    t15 = dot(t1.xyz, t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 163
    //RSQ
    t15 = inversesqrt(t15);
    //Instruction 164
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t15) * t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 165
    //MUL
    t5 = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 166
    //MAD

"!!GLSL#version 120

#ifdef VERTEX
uniform vec4 _ProjectionParams;



uniform vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform mat4 _TerrainEngineBendTree;
uniform vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform float _SquashAmount;
varying vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
void main ()
{
  vec4 tmpvar_1;
  vec4 pos_2;
  pos_2.w = gl_Vertex.w;
  pos_2.xyz = (gl_Vertex.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz);
  vec4 tmpvar_3;
  tmpvar_3.w = 0.0;
  tmpvar_3.xyz = pos_2.xyz;
  pos_2.xyz = mix (pos_2.xyz, (_TerrainEngineBendTree * tmpvar_3).xyz, gl_Color.www);
  vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_4.xyz = mix ((pos_2.xyz - (
    (dot (_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, pos_2.xyz) + _SquashPlaneNormal.w)
   * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz)), pos_2.xyz, vec3(_SquashAmount));
  pos_2 = tmpvar_4;
  mat3 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5[0] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_5[1] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_5[2] = gl_ModelViewMatrixInverseTranspose[2].xyz;
  tmpvar_1.xyz = normalize((tmpvar_5 * gl_Normal));
  tmpvar_1.w = -(((gl_ModelViewMatrix * tmpvar_4).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (gl_ModelViewProjectionMatrix * tmpvar_4);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
varying vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
void main ()
{

  vec2 enc_2;

  enc_3.y = tmpvar_4.y;
  enc_3.x = (tmpvar_4.x - (tmpvar_4.y * 0.003921569));
  enc_1.zw = enc_3;
  gl_FragData[0] = enc_1;
}


#endif
"

SubProgram "gles " {
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesColor;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform highp mat4 _TerrainEngineBendTree;
uniform highp vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform highp float _SquashAmount;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1 = _glesColor;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_2;
  highp vec4 pos_3;
  pos_3.w = _glesVertex.w;
  highp float alpha_4;
  alpha_4 = tmpvar_1.w;
  pos_3.xyz = (_glesVertex.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5.w = 0.0;
  tmpvar_5.xyz = pos_3.xyz;
  pos_3.xyz = mix (pos_3.xyz, (_TerrainEngineBendTree * tmpvar_5).xyz, vec3(alpha_4));
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_6.xyz = mix ((pos_3.xyz - (
    (dot (_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, pos_3.xyz) + _SquashPlaneNormal.w)
   * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz)), pos_3.xyz, vec3(_SquashAmount));
  pos_3 = tmpvar_6;
  highp mat3 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7[0] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_7[1] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_7[2] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz;
  tmpvar_2.xyz = normalize((tmpvar_7 * _glesNormal));
  tmpvar_2.w = -(((glstate_matrix_modelview0 * tmpvar_6).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (glstate_matrix_mvp * tmpvar_6);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = tmpvar_2;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;

uniform 	lowp vec4 _TreeInstanceColor;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform 	mat4 _TerrainEngineBendTree;
uniform 	vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform 	float _SquashAmount;
uniform 	vec3 _TreeBillboardCameraRight;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraUp;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraFront;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _TreeBillboardDistances;
uniform 	vec4 _Wind;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in lowp vec4 in_COLOR0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
highp vec3 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
highp float t2;
highp float t6;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 34
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz;
    //Instruction 35
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * _TerrainEngineBendTree[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 36
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 37
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 38
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-in_POSITION0.xyz) * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 39
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = in_COLOR0.www * t1.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 40
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 41
    //ADD
    t6 = t6 + _SquashPlaneNormal.w;
    //Instruction 42
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-vec3(t6)) * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz + t0.xyz;

SubProgram "gles " {
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesColor;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform highp mat4 _TerrainEngineBendTree;
uniform highp vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform highp float _SquashAmount;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1 = _glesColor;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_2;
  highp vec4 pos_3;
  pos_3.w = _glesVertex.w;
  highp float alpha_4;
  alpha_4 = tmpvar_1.w;
  pos_3.xyz = (_glesVertex.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5.w = 0.0;
  tmpvar_5.xyz = pos_3.xyz;
  pos_3.xyz = mix (pos_3.xyz, (_TerrainEngineBendTree * tmpvar_5).xyz, vec3(alpha_4));
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_6.xyz = mix ((pos_3.xyz - (
    (dot (_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, pos_3.xyz) + _SquashPlaneNormal.w)
   * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz)), pos_3.xyz, vec3(_SquashAmount));
  pos_3 = tmpvar_6;
  highp mat3 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7[0] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_7[1] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_7[2] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz;
  tmpvar_2.xyz = normalize((tmpvar_7 * _glesNormal));
  tmpvar_2.w = -(((glstate_matrix_modelview0 * tmpvar_6).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (glstate_matrix_mvp * tmpvar_6);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = _glesMultiTexCoord0.xy;
  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = tmpvar_2;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
uniform sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp float _Cutoff;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  mediump float alpha_2;
  lowp float tmpvar_3;
  tmpvar_3 = texture2D (_MainTex, xlv_TEXCOORD0).w;
  alpha_2 = tmpvar_3;
  mediump float x_4;
  x_4 = (alpha_2 - _Cutoff);
  if ((x_4 < 0.0)) {
    discard;
  };
  highp vec4 enc_5;
  highp vec2 enc_6;
  enc_6 = (xlv_TEXCOORD1.xy / (xlv_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0));
  enc_6 = (enc_6 / 1.7777);
  enc_6 = ((enc_6 * 0.5) + 0.5);
  enc_5.xy = enc_6;
  highp vec2 enc_7;
  highp vec2 tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = fract((vec2(1.0, 255.0) * xlv_TEXCOORD1.w));
  enc_7.y = tmpvar_8.y;
  enc_7.x = (tmpvar_8.x - (tmpvar_8.y * 0.003921569));
  enc_5.zw = enc_7;
  tmpvar_1 = enc_5;
  gl_FragData[0] = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
"
}

out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

highp vec4 t1;

highp float t6;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 106
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz;
    //Instruction 107
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * _TerrainEngineBendTree[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 108
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 109
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 110
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-in_POSITION0.xyz) * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 111
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = in_COLOR0.www * t1.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 112
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 113
    //ADD
    t6 = t6 + _SquashPlaneNormal.w;
    //Instruction 114
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-vec3(t6)) * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 115
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 116
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = vec3(_SquashAmount) * t0.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 117
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 118
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 119
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 120
    //ADD
    gl_Position = t1 + glstate_matrix_mvp[3];
    //Instruction 121
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 122
    //MUL
    t2 = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 123
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t0.x + t2;
    //Instruction 124
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 125
    //ADD
    t0.x = t0.x + glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z;
    //Instruction 126
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 127
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 128
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 129
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 130
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 131
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 132
    //RSQ
    t6 = inversesqrt(t6);
    //Instruction 133
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t6) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 134
    //RET
    return;
}

lowp float t10_0;
bool tb0;
mediump float t16_1;
highp vec2 t2;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 93
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    //Instruction 94
    //ADD
    t16_1 = t10_0 + (-_Cutoff);
    //Instruction 95
    //LT
    tb0 = t16_1<0.0;
    //Instruction 96
    //DISCARD
    if((int(tb0))!=0){discard;}
    //Instruction 97
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 98
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 99
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 100
    //MUL
    t2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 101
    //FRC
    t2.xy = fract(t2.xy);
    //Instruction 102
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t2.y) * 0.003922 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 103
    //MOV
    t0.w = t2.y;
    //Instruction 104
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 105
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif

void main()
{
    //Instruction 12
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz;
    //Instruction 13

    //Instruction 22
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = vec3(_SquashAmount) * t0.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 23
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 24
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 25

    //Instruction 26

    gl_Position = t1 + glstate_matrix_mvp[3];

    //MUL
    t2 = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 29
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t0.x + t2;
    //Instruction 30
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 31
    //ADD
    t0.x = t0.x + glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z;
    //Instruction 32
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 33
    //MOV

    //MUL

    //Instruction 35
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 36
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 37
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 38
    //RSQ
    t6 = inversesqrt(t6);
    //Instruction 39
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t6) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 40
    //RET
    return;
}

  tmpvar_3.w = 0.0;
  tmpvar_3.xyz = pos_2.xyz;

SubProgram "gles " {
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesColor;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeInstanceScale;
uniform highp mat4 _TerrainEngineBendTree;
uniform highp vec4 _SquashPlaneNormal;
uniform highp float _SquashAmount;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1 = _glesColor;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_2;
  highp vec4 pos_3;
  pos_3.w = _glesVertex.w;
  highp float alpha_4;
  alpha_4 = tmpvar_1.w;
  pos_3.xyz = (_glesVertex.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5.w = 0.0;
  tmpvar_5.xyz = pos_3.xyz;
  pos_3.xyz = mix (pos_3.xyz, (_TerrainEngineBendTree * tmpvar_5).xyz, vec3(alpha_4));
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_6.xyz = mix ((pos_3.xyz - (
    (dot (_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, pos_3.xyz) + _SquashPlaneNormal.w)
   * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz)), pos_3.xyz, vec3(_SquashAmount));
  pos_3 = tmpvar_6;
  highp mat3 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7[0] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz;
  tmpvar_7[1] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
  tmpvar_7[2] = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz;
  tmpvar_2.xyz = -(normalize((tmpvar_7 * _glesNormal)));
  tmpvar_2.w = -(((glstate_matrix_modelview0 * tmpvar_6).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (glstate_matrix_mvp * tmpvar_6);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = _glesMultiTexCoord0.xy;
  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = tmpvar_2;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
uniform sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp float _Cutoff;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  lowp float x_2;
  x_2 = (texture2D (_MainTex, xlv_TEXCOORD0).w - _Cutoff);
  if ((x_2 < 0.0)) {
    discard;
  };
  highp vec4 enc_3;
  highp vec2 enc_4;
  enc_4 = (xlv_TEXCOORD1.xy / (xlv_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0));
  enc_4 = (enc_4 / 1.7777);
  enc_4 = ((enc_4 * 0.5) + 0.5);
  enc_3.xy = enc_4;
  highp vec2 enc_5;
  highp vec2 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6 = fract((vec2(1.0, 255.0) * xlv_TEXCOORD1.w));
  enc_5.y = tmpvar_6.y;
  enc_5.x = (tmpvar_6.x - (tmpvar_6.y * 0.003921569));
  enc_3.zw = enc_5;
  tmpvar_1 = enc_3;
  gl_FragData[0] = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
"
}

in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in lowp vec4 in_COLOR0;
in highp vec4 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
highp vec3 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
highp float t2;
highp float t6;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 54
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz;
    //Instruction 55
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * _TerrainEngineBendTree[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 56
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 57
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 58
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-in_POSITION0.xyz) * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 59
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = in_COLOR0.www * t1.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 60
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 61
    //ADD
    t6 = t6 + _SquashPlaneNormal.w;
    //Instruction 62
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-vec3(t6)) * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 63
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 64
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = vec3(_SquashAmount) * t0.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 65
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 66
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 67
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 68
    //ADD
    gl_Position = t1 + glstate_matrix_mvp[3];
    //Instruction 69
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 70
    //MUL
    t2 = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 71
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t0.x + t2;
    //Instruction 72
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 73
    //ADD
    t0.x = t0.x + glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z;
    //Instruction 74
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 75
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 76
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 77
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 78
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 79
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 80
    //RSQ
    t6 = inversesqrt(t6);
    //Instruction 81
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = vec3(t6) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 82
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = (-t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 83
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif

lowp float t10_0;
bool tb0;
lowp float t10_1;
highp vec2 t2;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 41
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    //Instruction 42
    //ADD
    t10_1 = t10_0 + (-_Cutoff);
    //Instruction 43
    //LT
    tb0 = t10_1<0.0;
    //Instruction 44
    //DISCARD
    if((int(tb0))!=0){discard;}
    //Instruction 45
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 46
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 47
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 48
    //MUL
    t2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 49
    //FRC
    t2.xy = fract(t2.xy);
    //Instruction 50
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t2.y) * 0.003922 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 51
    //MOV
    t0.w = t2.y;
    //Instruction 52
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 53
    //RET
    return;
}

out vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

float t6;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 147
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz;
    //Instruction 148
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * _TerrainEngineBendTree[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 149
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 150
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = _TerrainEngineBendTree[2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 151
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-in_POSITION0.xyz) * _TreeInstanceScale.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 152
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = in_COLOR0.www * t1.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 153
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(_SquashPlaneNormal.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 154
    //ADD
    t6 = t6 + _SquashPlaneNormal.w;
    //Instruction 155
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = (-vec3(t6)) * _SquashPlaneNormal.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 156
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 157
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = vec3(_SquashAmount) * t0.xyz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 158
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 159
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 160
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 161
    //ADD
    gl_Position = t1 + glstate_matrix_mvp[3];
    //Instruction 162
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 163
    //MUL
    t2 = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 164
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t0.x + t2;
    //Instruction 165
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t0.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 166
    //ADD
    t0.x = t0.x + glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z;
    //Instruction 167
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 168
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 169
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 170
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 171
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 172
    //DP3
    t6 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 173
    //RSQ
    t6 = inversesqrt(t6);
    //Instruction 174
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = vec3(t6) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 175
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = (-t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 176
    //RET
    return;
}

    offsetz_5 = 0.0;

SubProgram "gles " {
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord1;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform highp vec3 _TreeBillboardCameraRight;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraUp;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraFront;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeBillboardCameraPos;
uniform highp vec4 _TreeBillboardDistances;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  highp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  tmpvar_1 = _glesMultiTexCoord0;
  highp vec2 tmpvar_2;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_3;
  highp vec4 pos_4;
  pos_4 = _glesVertex;
  highp vec2 offset_5;
  offset_5 = _glesMultiTexCoord1.xy;
  highp float offsetz_6;
  offsetz_6 = tmpvar_1.y;
  highp vec3 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7 = (_glesVertex.xyz - _TreeBillboardCameraPos.xyz);
  highp float tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = dot (tmpvar_7, tmpvar_7);
  if ((tmpvar_8 > _TreeBillboardDistances.x)) {
    offsetz_6 = 0.0;
    offset_5 = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
  };
  pos_4.xyz = (_glesVertex.xyz + (_TreeBillboardCameraRight * offset_5.x));
  pos_4.xyz = (pos_4.xyz + (_TreeBillboardCameraUp.xyz * mix (offset_5.y, offsetz_6, _TreeBillboardCameraPos.w)));
  pos_4.xyz = (pos_4.xyz + ((_TreeBillboardCameraFront.xyz * 
    abs(offset_5.x)
  ) * _TreeBillboardCameraUp.w));
  tmpvar_2.x = tmpvar_1.x;
  tmpvar_2.y = float((_glesMultiTexCoord0.y > 0.0));
  tmpvar_3.xyz = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
  tmpvar_3.w = -(((glstate_matrix_modelview0 * pos_4).z * _ProjectionParams.w));
  gl_Position = (glstate_matrix_mvp * pos_4);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = tmpvar_2;
  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = tmpvar_3;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
uniform sampler2D _MainTex;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_1;
  lowp float x_2;
  x_2 = (texture2D (_MainTex, xlv_TEXCOORD0).w - 0.001);
  if ((x_2 < 0.0)) {
    discard;
  };
  highp vec4 enc_3;
  highp vec2 enc_4;
  enc_4 = (xlv_TEXCOORD1.xy / (xlv_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0));
  enc_4 = (enc_4 / 1.7777);
  enc_4 = ((enc_4 * 0.5) + 0.5);
  enc_3.xy = enc_4;
  highp vec2 enc_5;
  highp vec2 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6 = fract((vec2(1.0, 255.0) * xlv_TEXCOORD1.w));
  enc_5.y = tmpvar_6.y;
  enc_5.x = (tmpvar_6.x - (tmpvar_6.y * 0.003921569));
  enc_3.zw = enc_5;
  tmpvar_1 = enc_3;
  gl_FragData[0] = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
"
}

SubProgram "gles " {

    offset_5 = vec2(0.0, 0.0);
  };

  highp vec4 tmpvar_18;
  tmpvar_18 = (tmpvar_17 * val_15);

highp float t15;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 115
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz + (-_CameraPosition.xyz);
    //Instruction 116
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 117
    //LT
    tb0 = _WaveAndDistance.w<t0.x;
    //Instruction 118
    //MOVC
    t0.xy = (bool(tb0)) ? vec2(0.0, 0.0) : in_TANGENT0.xy;
    //Instruction 119
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = t0.xxx * _CameraRight.xyzx.xyz + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    //Instruction 120
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = t0.yyy * _CameraUp.xyzx.xyz + t0.xzw;
    //Instruction 121
    //MUL
    t1.xy = t0.xz * _WaveAndDistance.yy;
    //Instruction 122
    //MUL
    t2 = t1.yyyy * vec4(0.006000, 0.020000, 0.020000, 0.050000);
    //Instruction 123
    //MAD
    t1 = t1.xxxx * vec4(0.012000, 0.020000, 0.060000, 0.024000) + t2;
    //Instruction 124
    //MAD
    t1 = _WaveAndDistance.xxxx * vec4(1.200000, 2.000000, 1.600000, 4.800000) + t1;
    //Instruction 125
    //FRC
    t1 = fract(t1);
    //Instruction 126
    //MAD
    t1 = t1 * vec4(6.408849, 6.408849, 6.408849, 6.408849) + vec4(-3.141593, -3.141593, -3.141593, -3.141593);
    //Instruction 127
    //MUL
    t2 = t1 * t1;
    //Instruction 128
    //MUL
    t3 = t1 * t2;
    //Instruction 129
    //MAD
    t1 = t3 * vec4(-0.161616, -0.161616, -0.161616, -0.161616) + t1;
    //Instruction 130
    //MUL
    t3 = t2 * t3;
    //Instruction 131
    //MUL
    t2 = t2 * t3;
    //Instruction 132
    //MAD
    t1 = t3 * vec4(0.008333, 0.008333, 0.008333, 0.008333) + t1;
    //Instruction 133
    //MAD
    t1 = t2 * vec4(-0.000198, -0.000198, -0.000198, -0.000198) + t1;
    //Instruction 134
    //MUL
    t1 = t1 * t1;
    //Instruction 135
    //MUL
    t1 = t1 * t1;
    //Instruction 136
    //MUL
    t2 = t1 * in_TANGENT0.yyyy;
    //Instruction 137
    //DP4
    t15 = dot(t1, vec4(0.674200, 0.674200, 0.269680, 0.134840));
    //Instruction 138
    //MUL
    t15 = t15 * 0.700000;
    //Instruction 139
    //DP4
    t1.x = dot(t2, vec4(0.024000, 0.040000, -0.120000, 0.096000));
    //Instruction 140
    //DP4
    t1.z = dot(t2, vec4(0.006000, 0.020000, -0.020000, 0.100000));
    //Instruction 141
    //MAD
    t0.xz = (-t1.xz) * _WaveAndDistance.zz + t0.xz;
    //Instruction 142
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 143
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 144
    //MAD
    t1 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 145
    //MAD
    gl_Position = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t1;
    //Instruction 146
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 147
    //MAD
    t1.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t0.x + t1.x;
    //Instruction 148
    //MAD
    t1.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t0.z + t1.x;
    //Instruction 149
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-_CameraPosition.xyz);
    //Instruction 150
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 151
    //ADD
    t0.x = (-t0.x) + _WaveAndDistance.w;
    //Instruction 152
    //DP2
    t0.x = dot(_CameraPosition.ww, t0.xx);
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 153
    //MOV
    vs_COLOR0.w = t0.x;
    //Instruction 154
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z * in_POSITION0.w + t1.x;
    //Instruction 155
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 156
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 157
    //ADD
    t10_4.xyz = _WavingTint.xyz + vec3(-0.500000, -0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 158
    //MAD
    t10_4.xyz = vec3(t15) * t10_4.xyz + vec3(0.500000, 0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 159
    //MUL
    t10_4.xyz = t10_4.xyz * in_COLOR0.xyz;
    //Instruction 160
    //MUL
    vs_COLOR0.xyz = t10_4.xyz * vec3(2.000000, 2.000000, 2.000000);
    //Instruction 161
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 162
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 163
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 164
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 165
    //DP3
    t15 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 166
    //RSQ
    t15 = inversesqrt(t15);
    //Instruction 167
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t15) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 168
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
lowp float t10_0;
bool tb0;
lowp float t10_1;
highp vec2 t2;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 102
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    //Instruction 103
    //MAD
    t10_1 = t10_0 * vs_COLOR0.w + (-_Cutoff);
    //Instruction 104
    //LT
    tb0 = t10_1<0.0;
    //Instruction 105
    //DISCARD
    if((int(tb0))!=0){discard;}
    //Instruction 106
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 107
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 108
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 109
    //MUL
    t2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 110
    //FRC
    t2.xy = fract(t2.xy);
    //Instruction 111
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t2.y) * 0.003922 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 112
    //MOV
    t0.w = t2.y;
    //Instruction 113
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 114
    //RET
    return;
}

in  vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in  vec4 in_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec4 in_COLOR0;
out vec4 vs_COLOR0;
out vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
vec4 t0;
bool tb0;
vec4 t1;
vec4 t2;
vec4 t3;
float t12;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 85
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz + (-_CameraPosition.xyz);
    //Instruction 86
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 87
    //LT
    tb0 = _WaveAndDistance.w<t0.x;
    //Instruction 88
    //MOVC
    t0.xy = (bool(tb0)) ? vec2(0.0, 0.0) : in_TANGENT0.xy;
    //Instruction 89
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = t0.xxx * _CameraRight.xyzx.xyz + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    //Instruction 90
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = t0.yyy * _CameraUp.xyzx.xyz + t0.xzw;
    //Instruction 91
    //MUL
    t1.xy = t0.xz * _WaveAndDistance.yy;
    //Instruction 92
    //MUL
    t2 = t1.yyyy * vec4(0.006000, 0.020000, 0.020000, 0.050000);
    //Instruction 93
    //MAD
    t1 = t1.xxxx * vec4(0.012000, 0.020000, 0.060000, 0.024000) + t2;
    //Instruction 94
    //MAD
    t1 = _WaveAndDistance.xxxx * vec4(1.200000, 2.000000, 1.600000, 4.800000) + t1;
    //Instruction 95
    //FRC
    t1 = fract(t1);
    //Instruction 96
    //MAD
    t1 = t1 * vec4(6.408849, 6.408849, 6.408849, 6.408849) + vec4(-3.141593, -3.141593, -3.141593, -3.141593);
    //Instruction 97
    //MUL
    t2 = t1 * t1;
    //Instruction 98

    t3 = t1 * t2;
    //Instruction 99

    t1 = t3 * vec4(-0.161616, -0.161616, -0.161616, -0.161616) + t1;
    //Instruction 100
    //MUL
    t3 = t2 * t3;
    //Instruction 101
    //MUL
    t2 = t2 * t3;
    //Instruction 102
    //MAD
    t1 = t3 * vec4(0.008333, 0.008333, 0.008333, 0.008333) + t1;
    //Instruction 103
    //MAD
    t1 = t2 * vec4(-0.000198, -0.000198, -0.000198, -0.000198) + t1;
    //Instruction 104
    //MUL
    t1 = t1 * t1;
    //Instruction 105
    //MUL
    t1 = t1 * t1;
    //Instruction 106
    //MUL
    t2 = t1 * in_TANGENT0.yyyy;

    //MAD

    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 121
    //ADD
    t0.x = (-t0.x) + _WaveAndDistance.w;
    //Instruction 122
    //DP2

    vs_COLOR0.w = clamp(vs_COLOR0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 123
    //MAD

    //Instruction 125

    vs_COLOR0.xyz = t0.xyz * in_COLOR0.xyz;

lowp float t10_0;
bool tb0;
lowp float t10_1;
highp vec2 t2;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 138
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).w;
    //Instruction 139
    //MAD
    t10_1 = t10_0 * vs_COLOR0.w + (-_Cutoff);
    //Instruction 140
    //LT
    tb0 = t10_1<0.0;
    //Instruction 141
    //DISCARD
    if((int(tb0))!=0){discard;}
    //Instruction 142
    //ADD
    t0.x = vs_TEXCOORD1.z + 1.0;
    //Instruction 143
    //DIV
    t0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.xy / t0.xx;
    //Instruction 144
    //MAD
    t0.xy = t0.xy * vec2(0.281262, 0.281262) + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 145
    //MUL
    t2.xy = vs_TEXCOORD1.ww * vec2(1.0, 255.000000);
    //Instruction 146
    //FRC
    t2.xy = fract(t2.xy);
    //Instruction 147
    //MAD
    t0.z = (-t2.y) * 0.003922 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 148
    //MOV
    t0.w = t2.y;
    //Instruction 149
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 150
    //RET
    return;
}

"

out vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;

float t9;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 184
    //MUL
    t0.xy = in_POSITION0.xz * _WaveAndDistance.yy;
    //Instruction 185
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * vec4(0.006000, 0.020000, 0.020000, 0.050000);
    //Instruction 186
    //MAD
    t0 = t0.xxxx * vec4(0.012000, 0.020000, 0.060000, 0.024000) + t1;
    //Instruction 187
    //MAD
    t0 = _WaveAndDistance.xxxx * vec4(1.200000, 2.000000, 1.600000, 4.800000) + t0;
    //Instruction 188
    //FRC
    t0 = fract(t0);
    //Instruction 189
    //MAD
    t0 = t0 * vec4(6.408849, 6.408849, 6.408849, 6.408849) + vec4(-3.141593, -3.141593, -3.141593, -3.141593);
    //Instruction 190
    //MUL
    t1 = t0 * t0;
    //Instruction 191
    //MUL
    t2 = t0 * t1;
    //Instruction 192
    //MAD
    t0 = t2 * vec4(-0.161616, -0.161616, -0.161616, -0.161616) + t0;
    //Instruction 193
    //MUL
    t2 = t1 * t2;
    //Instruction 194
    //MUL
    t1 = t1 * t2;
    //Instruction 195
    //MAD
    t0 = t2 * vec4(0.008333, 0.008333, 0.008333, 0.008333) + t0;
    //Instruction 196
    //MAD
    t0 = t1 * vec4(-0.000198, -0.000198, -0.000198, -0.000198) + t0;
    //Instruction 197
    //MUL
    t0 = t0 * t0;
    //Instruction 198
    //MUL
    t0 = t0 * t0;
    //Instruction 199
    //MUL
    t1.x = in_COLOR0.w * _WaveAndDistance.z;
    //Instruction 200
    //MUL
    t1 = t0 * t1.xxxx;
    //Instruction 201
    //DP4
    t0.x = dot(t0, vec4(0.674200, 0.674200, 0.269680, 0.134840));
    //Instruction 202
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * 0.700000;
    //Instruction 203
    //DP4
    t2.x = dot(t1, vec4(0.024000, 0.040000, -0.120000, 0.096000));
    //Instruction 204
    //DP4
    t2.z = dot(t1, vec4(0.006000, 0.020000, -0.020000, 0.100000));
    //Instruction 205
    //MAD
    t1.xz = (-t2.xz) * _WaveAndDistance.zz + in_POSITION0.xz;
    //Instruction 206
    //MUL
    t2 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 207
    //MAD
    t2 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * t1.xxxx + t2;
    //Instruction 208
    //MAD
    t2 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * t1.zzzz + t2;
    //Instruction 209
    //MAD
    gl_Position = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t2;
    //Instruction 210
    //ADD
    t3.xyz = _WavingTint.xyz + vec3(-0.500000, -0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 211
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = t0.xxx * t3.xyz + vec3(0.500000, 0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 212
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz * in_COLOR0.xyz;
    //Instruction 213
    //ADD
    vs_COLOR0.xyz = t0.xyz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 214
    //MOV
    t1.y = in_POSITION0.y;
    //Instruction 215
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t1.xyz + (-_CameraPosition.xyz);
    //Instruction 216
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 217
    //ADD
    t0.x = (-t0.x) + _WaveAndDistance.w;
    //Instruction 218
    //ADD
    t0.x = t0.x + t0.x;
    //Instruction 219
    //MUL
    vs_COLOR0.w = t0.x * _CameraPosition.w;
    vs_COLOR0.w = clamp(vs_COLOR0.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 220
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 221
    //MUL
    t0.x = in_POSITION0.y * glstate_matrix_modelview0[1].z;
    //Instruction 222
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[0].z * t1.x + t0.x;
    //Instruction 223
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[2].z * t1.z + t0.x;
    //Instruction 224
    //MAD
    t0.x = glstate_matrix_modelview0[3].z * in_POSITION0.w + t0.x;
    //Instruction 225
    //MUL
    t0.x = t0.x * _ProjectionParams.w;
    //Instruction 226
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 227
    //MUL
    t0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 228
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 229
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 230
    //DP3
    t9 = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 231
    //RSQ
    t9 = inversesqrt(t9);
    //Instruction 232
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = vec3(t9) * t0.xyz;
    //Instruction 233
    //RET
    return;
}
